<div id="review_515154020" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/515154020" />
    <a title="The BookChick " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6190526-the-bookchick"><img alt="The BookChick " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1546023730p2/6190526.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/515154020?book_show_action=true">Jan 23, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="The BookChick " class="user" itemprop="url" name="The BookChick " href="/user/show/6190526-the-bookchick">The BookChick </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6190526-the-bookchick?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6190526-the-bookchick?shelf=fifty-shades-ish">fifty-shades-ish</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6190526-the-bookchick?shelf=never-read-again">never-read-again</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6190526-the-bookchick?shelf=netgalley-review-book">netgalley-review-book</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6190526-the-bookchick?shelf=don-t-even-think-about-it">don-t-even-think-about-it</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6190526-the-bookchick?shelf=what-in-the-world">what-in-the-world</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6190526-the-bookchick?shelf=porn-on-paper">porn-on-paper</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6190526-the-bookchick?shelf=1-star-read">1-star-read</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer515154020" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6511179129948074605"><b>My Rating:</b> ❤<blockquote> FAIL: The characteristics of a 1 star book include: the story failed to hold my attention; it didn’t have interesting characters; the storyline was trite or contrived; and/or their was extremely crude behavior/language. I would not never recommend the book to anyone.</blockquote><b>Book Description:</b><br/>An ambitious intern. A perfectionist executive. And a whole lot of name calling. Discover the story that garnered more than two million reads online.<br/><br/>Whip-smart, hardworking, and on her way to an MBA, Chl</span>
  <span id="freeText6511179129948074605" style="display:none"><b>My Rating:</b> ❤<blockquote> FAIL: The characteristics of a 1 star book include: the story failed to hold my attention; it didn’t have interesting characters; the storyline was trite or contrived; and/or their was extremely crude behavior/language. I would not never recommend the book to anyone.</blockquote><b>Book Description:</b><br>An ambitious intern. A perfectionist executive. And a whole lot of name calling. Discover the story that garnered more than two million reads online.<br><br>Whip-smart, hardworking, and on her way to an MBA, Chloe Mills has only one problem: her boss, Bennett Ryan. He’s exacting, blunt, inconsiderate—and completely irresistible. A Beautiful Bastard.<br><br>Bennett has returned to Chicago from France to take a vital role in his family’s massive media business. He never expected that the assistant who’d been helping him from abroad was the gorgeous, innocently provocative—completely infuriating—creature he now has to see every day. Despite the rumors, he’s never been one for a workplace hookup. But Chloe’s so tempting he’s willing to bend the rules—or outright smash them—if it means he can have her. All over the office.<br><br>As their appetites for one another increase to a breaking point, Bennett and Chloe must decide exactly what they’re willing to lose in order to win each other. Originally only available online as The Office by tby789—and garnering over two million reads on fan fiction sites—Beautiful Bastard has been extensively updated for re-release.<br><br><b>Page Count:</b> 320 pages<br><br><b>Immediate Post-Read Reaction:</b><br>SMH...This book was literally porn on paper. No romance. No build up. No story. Just sex...sex...and more sex.<br><br><b>My Thoughts:</b><br><i>This book was provided by Net Galley and Gallery Books for an honest review.</i> Fair warning that this review is going to real, raw, and honest. Brutally so.<br><br>There are a few times that you read books that are so epic that they leave you speechless. <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16102004.Beautiful_Bastard__Beautiful_Bastard___1_" title="Beautiful Bastard (Beautiful Bastard, #1) by Christina Lauren" rel="nofollow noopener">Beautiful Bastard</a> was such a book. It was epically painful to read and I had to force myself to read to the end. Honestly, the only reason I did finish it was because I committed to complete this review and that required finishing the "story" and I use the word "story" in its loosest sense. <i>Beautiful Bastard</i> was really and truly porn on paper. At 5% into the story Bennett is fingering Chloe in the conference room. <i>*Huh! What?!?!? Did I miss a page or 100?*</i> I was truly speechless. 5% in and BAM! The rest of the story follows in a similar fashion. Bennett and Chloe absolutely loathe one another. "B!tc#" from Bennett and "a$$hole" from Chloe flies fast, furious, and often between the two characters. Yet...yet...they go at it like rabbits at every opportunity. Verbal sparring is their foreplay and they do it often. She is "getting wet" and he is "getting hard" all the time. Did I say all the time? Because I mean...ALL. THE. TIME. Their trysts occur on a conference table, in an elevator, the parking garage, a dressing room...<i>and oh YAY!!!...joy of all joys</i>...finally, a bed. <br><br>There is <b>never</b> a moment in the story when I think, "Hmm, these two actually love each other." Oh yeah, they <i>say</i> it and Bennett even gets to the point where he calls Chloe "baby" but I never believe it or feel any love from them because of their actions. At 85% into the story Bennett is still regarding Chloe as a shrew. And he loves her?!?!? Really?!?!? They were petty and juvenile and their relationship was toxic. I regarded them both as <i>sexual masochists.</i> <br><br>Chloe is incensed because Bennett offers her an open line of credit at a lingerie store. Oh, did I forget to mention that Bennett has a panty fetish? He likes ripping them off of Chloe. I counted seven times in the story where panty ripping occurred. But, I digress...back to Chloe being incensed <i>*sigh and yawn*</i>. She screams at Bennett, <b>
  <i>Do you think I'm some kind of whore?</i>
</b>And I kid you not, three pages later, this is Chloe: <b>
  <i>"God, I moaned, wrapping my leg around him and digging my heel into his thigh.</i>
</b> This particular tête-à-tête happens in the parking garage. My immediate thought after reading this was: "Hmmm, public sex?!?!? If it moans like a whore and grinds like a whore...it's a whore, right?"<br><br>I know that many people took issue with this book because it was first written as fanfic. Honestly, I am one of the rare readers that doesn't have a problem with fanfiction. I regard fanfiction the same way I regard remade films. I can still enjoy them even though they have been done before. Really. The <i>King Kong</i> movie has been remade many different times but each time it was a box office sensation so why can't that be the case with books, right? No...my issue with <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16102004.Beautiful_Bastard__Beautiful_Bastard___1_" title="Beautiful Bastard (Beautiful Bastard, #1) by Christina Lauren" rel="nofollow noopener">Beautiful Bastard</a> did not stem from its fanfic origins but from the fact that it was totally pointless. The characters were uninteresting and moronic and the story was the equivalent of watching a porn film. There was no climax to the story at all..it just was! The beginning, middle, and end just fell below flat...except for the sex. Steamy yes. But after the <i>nth</i> time it just became banal.<br><br>My apologies to the authors on this review because I can appreciate their writing effort. But, a bunch of sex strung together doth not a story make. I would never read or recommend this story to anyone. Quite the opposite actually. My public service announcement on this one is: <b>"Run away...FAST!</b><br><br>Sadly, this is one of the few books that I can certifiably say that I hated both the characters and the story. And notice that this is book 1 of x. There's more?!?!? <i>*Sigh*</i><br><br><b>Reading Time:</b> 4.5 Hours<br><br><b>Visit The BookChick Blog</b> <a href="http://bookchickwithkick.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380388474i/748995.jpg" alt=" photo 480761_117447861780253_1600570465_n_zps49e00d53.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="6511179129948074605" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer892254362" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16632691107374070564"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1397668840i/9308896.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>***Calling all ye SMUT FANS***</b><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1397724335ra/9318043.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I have a new book boyfriend to add to my list. Meet <b>Bennet Ryna</b>, a beautiful bastard who will make your panties drop if he doesn't rip them off first! He's cocky, a stud in the bedroom and absolutely divine! What more could a girl ask for then? Did I mention the fact that he's gorgeous too?<br/><br/><b>
  <u>I grudgingly admit</u>
</b><br/>One of the few heroines that I loved reading it about. She an alpha female, but she and Ryan make it work! I could harp on about what else I like about her b</span>
  <span id="freeText16632691107374070564" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1397668840i/9308896.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>***Calling all ye SMUT FANS***</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1397724335ra/9318043.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I have a new book boyfriend to add to my list. Meet <b>Bennet Ryna</b>, a beautiful bastard who will make your panties drop if he doesn't rip them off first! He's cocky, a stud in the bedroom and absolutely divine! What more could a girl ask for then? Did I mention the fact that he's gorgeous too?<br><br><b>
  <u>I grudgingly admit</u>
</b><br>One of the few heroines that I loved reading it about. She an alpha female, but she and Ryan make it work! I could harp on about what else I like about her but that's not how I roll lol!<br><br>Once again, I need to stress that this book is a <b>SMUT FEST</b>, when the characters in this book feel they feel strongly. So when they're sad, they f*ck, when they're happy, they f*ck, and just for they heck of it they still f*ck! <br><br><b>
  <u>A little about the story</u>
</b><br>Chloe, is Bennet's personal assistant they have a weird relationship. They basically hate each other but they when it comes to business they work like a well oiled machine. Until one day... Bennett snaps he's been hiding his lust for Chloe since he first me her, but when she reciprocates they attraction rises to dangerous heights and the sex is positively electric!<br><br>And so begins a relationship full of sexual gratification. Heated looks, stolen kisses, and some very delicious groping! These two will have sex wherever they can, if they opportunity makes itself known, then trust me they'll use it!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1397668840i/9308897._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Intercourse. Penetration.</b> That's what it's all about! I was looking for a smutty read, and that's what I got! I haven't mentioned how funny this book was, it was hilarious and I'm not a huge fan of humour it tends to dim the alphaness (yes, I just made that word up) of the male character. I don't want to read about a comedic alpha male. And trust me Bennett Ryan is most definitely an alpha male!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1381942286ra/5452785.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I'm quite impressed with this series so I will definitely continue the rest!</span>

    <a title="• Lisa •" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11963959-lisa"><img alt="• Lisa •" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1576172089p2/11963959.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/452173149?book_show_action=true">Nov 09, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="• Lisa •" class="user" itemprop="url" name="• Lisa •" href="/user/show/11963959-lisa">• Lisa •</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer452173149" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12437274874743922039">HELLO Mr Ryan wink, wink ...<br/><br/>This was not everyone's cup of tea, but I LOVED it. <br/><br/>The start of the book was great -mean boss, hardworking assistant and a boardroom full of chemistry - (literally), nothing grabs me more than a book about two people who dislike each other BUT are unable to resist. <br/><br/>The story did have a predictability factor, but hey ho it's what I signed up for. The book most certainly was a romp FEST, I'm not sure a chapter went by that didn't include some sort of bodily fluid excha</span>
  <span id="freeText12437274874743922039" style="display:none">HELLO Mr Ryan wink, wink ...<br><br>This was not everyone's cup of tea, but I LOVED it. <br><br>The start of the book was great -mean boss, hardworking assistant and a boardroom full of chemistry - (literally), nothing grabs me more than a book about two people who dislike each other BUT are unable to resist. <br><br>The story did have a predictability factor, but hey ho it's what I signed up for. The book most certainly was a romp FEST, I'm not sure a chapter went by that didn't include some sort of bodily fluid exchange , and yes maybe the authors could have included a bit more story telling, but I enjoyed the book from beginning to end.<br><br>So, for some readers you may think this book is ALL about the alpha male, and while this may be partly true it's not the whole picture, this book includes a heroine who knows what she wants and when, and I loved it.<br><br>Mr Bennett Ryan, ruthless business man known for his straight forward ways and as the book title suggests, he has been given the label of 'beautiful bastard'. Cleverly through the dual POV the reader is able to see that there is more than meets the eye with this gorgeous hero, and I enjoyed his character thoroughly. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397072i/765901._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="500" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Chloe Mills, what a welcome surprise, sassy, witty and with one liners that put a smile on my face, she is definitely a female heroine that I greatly enjoyed.<br><br>All in all this book had my heart racing and brought more than one smile to my face. I found it unputdownable and I was surprised at the mixed reviews. <br><br>This book had the 'i cant wait for spare time to read this book again' factor. You won't find anything shocking or different about this read, but if smut loving is your thing then i'm sure you will enjoy. As for moi this was right up my street, definitely my cup of tea and all of that ...<br><br>4 stars.</span>

<div id="review_2244173816" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2244173816" />
    <a title="Nissa | Of Pens and Pages Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/41356020-nissa-of-pens-and-pages-book-blog"><img alt="Nissa | Of Pens and Pages Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1465210954p2/41356020.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2244173816?book_show_action=true">Jan 05, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Nissa | Of Pens and Pages Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Nissa | Of Pens and Pages Book Blog" href="/user/show/41356020-nissa-of-pens-and-pages-book-blog">Nissa | Of Pens and Pages Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Audiobook 9781442363724" href="/book/show/17164461-beautiful-bastard">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/41356020-nissa-of-pens-and-pages-book-blog?shelf=audiobook">audiobook</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/41356020-nissa-of-pens-and-pages-book-blog?shelf=office-romance">office-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/41356020-nissa-of-pens-and-pages-book-blog?shelf=forbidden-romance">forbidden-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/41356020-nissa-of-pens-and-pages-book-blog?shelf=hate-to-love">hate-to-love</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/41356020-nissa-of-pens-and-pages-book-blog?shelf=adult-romance">adult-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/41356020-nissa-of-pens-and-pages-book-blog?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/41356020-nissa-of-pens-and-pages-book-blog?shelf=boss-employee">boss-employee</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/41356020-nissa-of-pens-and-pages-book-blog?shelf=dual-pov">dual-pov</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2244173816" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12146606494865572365"><b>Overall Rating:</b> 4 stars!<br/><b>Story Rating:</b> 3.5 stars!<br/><b>Performance Rating:</b> 5 stars!<br/><br/><b>STORY OVERVIEW AND REVIEW:</b><br/><br/>A genuine hate to love story, and lots of sex in between. Chloe Mills, an intern and MBA student, has been close to the Ryan family since she started working in their company a few year ago. The only one she can't seem to get along with is her current boss, Bennett Ryan, who recently moved back from France. As handsome as he is, she has no desire to ever jump on the Bennett Ryan wagon...until on</span>
  <span id="freeText12146606494865572365" style="display:none"><b>Overall Rating:</b> 4 stars!<br /><b>Story Rating:</b> 3.5 stars!<br /><b>Performance Rating:</b> 5 stars!<br /><br /><b>STORY OVERVIEW AND REVIEW:</b><br /><br />A genuine hate to love story, and lots of sex in between. Chloe Mills, an intern and MBA student, has been close to the Ryan family since she started working in their company a few year ago. The only one she can't seem to get along with is her current boss, Bennett Ryan, who recently moved back from France. As handsome as he is, she has no desire to ever jump on the Bennett Ryan wagon...until one encounter started their physical relationship. She still hates his guts and she's pretty sure he hates hers, but they can't seem to get enough of what they're doing.<br /><br />I enjoyed it well enough, but I have to admit this book had too much sex in it that I couldn't really fully see where hate turned into love. And all that panty-ripping. That's gotta hurt, I swear. It's like a reverse wedgie. He literally rips her panties every time they sleep together; it's come to a point that Bennett decided to open a credit line for Chloe at a lingerie store. Still, I don't know why but I'm already attached to this series. So much that I already bought the next books.<br /><br /><b>WHAT DID YOU LIKE ABOUT THE AUDIOBOOK?</b><br /><br />I usually don't enjoy an audiobook with only one narrator when a story is told in two POVs, but Grace Grant might be the exception to the rule. I was so into the audiobook that eventually, I forgot it was narrated by one person only. There was enough feeling in each depiction, and the narrator sure knew how to lay on thick the chemistry and sexual tension between herself and... herself. I'm gonna have to look for other audiobooks narrated by her. The pacing was just right and her voice was pleasant to listen to. I'm a pretty satisfied reader. <br /><br /><b>WOULD YOU RECOMMEND THIS AUDIOBOOK TO A FRIEND? IF SO, WHY?</b><br /><br />The story overall is fun, sexy, and easy to listen to. If you're looking for an entertaining and steamy audiobook with a great narrator who manages to wow the listener with her skills in perfectly acting out the two POVs, you'll enjoy listening to <i>Beautiful Bastard</i>.<br /><br /><b>Tropes:</b> Hate to Love, Office Romance, Forbidden Romance<br /><b>POV:</b> First Person, Dual POV<br /><b>Standalone:</b> Yes<br /><br /><a href="http://ofpensandpages.com" rel="nofollow noopener"> Blog</a> | <a href="http://facebook.com/ofpensandpages" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook</a> | <a href="http://twitter.com/ofpensandpages" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> | <a href="http://instagram.com/ofpensandpages" rel="nofollow noopener">Instagram</a></span>

  <span id="freeText16493775043745504651" style="display:none">Warning: 75% of this book is graphic erotica. Brain cells could be lost. <br /><br />What makes up the other 25%? <br /><br />In-depth revelations about tortured childhoods and abusive exes? Uh..no. <br /><br />Heart-pounding, bad-guy-slaying action? Definitely not. <br /><br />Daytime soap-opera office drama? Bingo. <br /><br />Then why the hell would I rate it five stars? Maybe this reviewer is just a perv who enjoys the boardroom table, cafe bathroom, elevator, parking garage, office desk, anywhere-but-a-bedroom sex. Really, this story is just boners and wet spots on a beautiful-bastard-vs-beautiful-bitch scale, which is still just boners and wet spots. <br /><br />Amidst all the balls-deep wall banging, I was drawn to the beautiful bitch, Chloe. For all the romances out there gravitating around bombastic billionaires, a rare few offer a heroine who can roar fiercely enough to blow back the leading asshole's perfectly manicured hair. Chloe made this pretentious bastard look like a kitten...a kitten you'll want to stroke and fondle. <br /><br />Chloe's an unintentional femme fatale and her empowered lip service--while most often over-reactive--might have some women fist pumping the air. While reading, you don't have to suffer an addle-brained heroine, ulcer-inducing jealousy, or soul-bleeding torment. In all the ways a book can torture you, this one doesn't try. It's simply a perverse pleasure. One that is panty-sniffingly creepy, stupefyingly shallow, and boldly sex-charged in a tawdry yet unable-to-put-the-book-down way. Sweet baby Jesus on Christmas, I enjoyed it. What's that say about me?<br /><br />***ARC by courtesy of Simon &amp; Schuster via Edelweiss in exchange for honest feedback.***</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer11724714286988283714">Not sure where to start with this one... It was entertaining and funny, and there were some hot scenes! <br/><br/>We start with Miss. Chloe Mills, an intern getting her MBA. Her boss is Mr. Bennett Ryan. Chloe has worked for Bennett for about 9 months. She has worked for his father's company for much longer than that, and is friendly with the Ryan family. Except for Bennett. They work well together, but they don’t really get a long. Mr. Ryan is seriously good looking, but also an ass.<br/><b> If only he would kee</b></span>
  <span id="freeText11724714286988283714" style="display:none">Not sure where to start with this one... It was entertaining and funny, and there were some hot scenes! <br><br>We start with Miss. Chloe Mills, an intern getting her MBA. Her boss is Mr. Bennett Ryan. Chloe has worked for Bennett for about 9 months. She has worked for his father's company for much longer than that, and is friendly with the Ryan family. Except for Bennett. They work well together, but they don’t really get a long. Mr. Ryan is seriously good looking, but also an ass.<br><b> If only he would keep his mouth shut, he’d be perfect.</b><br><br>The first half of the book is a ton of this....<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1505779953i/23959189.jpg" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Followed by even more of this...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1505779953i/23959187.jpg" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>and this....<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1505779953i/23959186.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>and more of this...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1505779953i/23959190.jpg" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Chloe and Bennett would fight, and screw, and fight, and screw... repeat repeat repeat. I wasn't sure exactly where the story was going during the first 30 or 40%... Luckily, after the first half, I started to really like the characters, especially Bennett. I have a thing for hot jerks and that’s exactly what he was! The dual pov's were great, I loved getting in both of the characters heads. Chloe and Bennett tried to stay away from each other, but they just couldn’t seem to keep their hands off of each other. <br><br><b>I felt possessive over her. Not in a romantic sort of way, but in a ‘hit her over the head, drag her off by the hair and fuck her” way.</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1505779953i/23959188.jpg" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Some of the sex scenes were a little ridiculous, the dialouge between the two of them cracked me up. But there were some that were some really hot. And for some reason, the pantie hoarding thing just made me laugh!<br><b>“And I tear lingerie” I pushed a curl off his forehead. “And hoard it. Don’t forget the creepy hoarding.”</b><br><br>Overall, this was an enjoyable read, it was a fun ride. I didn’t love it, but I didn’t hate it. I wish there was a little more ‘story’ and the ending felt a little rushed, but I was happy there was no cliff hanger! Woohoo! I really liked Bennett so I’m sure I will be reading book 2- as long as there is more Bennett! If you’re looking for a quick, steamy, fun read- This is for you! <br><br><i>This ARC was provided by NetGalley and Gallery Books</i></span>

<div id="review_2513632781" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2513632781" />
    <a title="Whitney Atkinson" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14457130-whitney-atkinson"><img alt="Whitney Atkinson" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1550868411p2/14457130.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2513632781?book_show_action=true">Jan 17, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Whitney Atkinson" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Whitney Atkinson" href="/user/show/14457130-whitney-atkinson">Whitney Atkinson</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14457130-whitney-atkinson?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14457130-whitney-atkinson?shelf=read-in-2019">read-in-2019</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14457130-whitney-atkinson?shelf=smutty">smutty</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2513632781" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12213333276191965236">I'm a huge fan of Christina Lauren; in fact, I would argue that they dominate the adult romance genre. However, I only bought this book with the intention to hate-read it. Although I love Christina Lauren's books now, I was convinced this would be miserable since it literally originated as Twilight fanfiction. But here's the thing... it wasn't that bad.<br/><br/>This book has a robust list of pros and cons, and I will start off with a huge disclaimer that I think I gave this book more credit than it deser</span>
  <span id="freeText12213333276191965236" style="display:none">I'm a huge fan of Christina Lauren; in fact, I would argue that they dominate the adult romance genre. However, I only bought this book with the intention to hate-read it. Although I love Christina Lauren's books now, I was convinced this would be miserable since it literally originated as Twilight fanfiction. But here's the thing... it wasn't that bad.<br /><br />This book has a robust list of pros and cons, and I will start off with a huge disclaimer that I think I gave this book more credit than it deserves just because I'm familiar with the authors and I like their other books and how they handle characters and relationships. Still, this book was heavy on some questionable qualities like the overprotective man who doesn't want to be with the main girl but also doesn't want her with anyone else. This book is a typical romance with a rude, demanding male character, so jumping into this and seeing the male character act so awful wasn't shocking at all. He did and said a lot of dumb stuff, which also wasn't shocking at all.<br /><br />What I didn't anticipate was how the female character consistently and thoroughly called him out on every single one of his gross actions, thus throwing those gross words or actions under intense scrutiny instead of brushing it under the rug as many other romances do. The main character isn't some meek character that lets the male love interest walk all over her. She stands her ground and is courageous enough to confront when she's being mistreated, and it put her and this seemingly macho and disgusting man on equal footing. By the end, although the male character said gross things to her and made questionable moves, I found that I couldn't hate him because he schooled himself to never do anything she wasn't comfortable with, and stop thinking and acting like he owned her. Because of that awareness in using such a problematic trope of the asshole boss, it didn't have me running for the hills like I anticipated (even though it was far from flawless or completely healthy). <br /><br />You can also tell that this is one of Christina Lauren's early works because there's not nearly enough description of the characters' lives. This basically is just a highlight reel of whenever these two characters exist on the page together, so there are no details about their home life or the mundane things the characters do to pass the time when they're not with their lovers, which I think are good buffers in their other books. Essentially, this book has sex in every single chapter with brooding<br />inner monologue interspersed, which made it so addicting as a romance book but a bit vapid as a fleshed out storyline. You could definitely locate its inspiration from Twilight, but I also think it was pretty original. I especially enjoyed the commentary on women in the business world and gender roles in the workplace, especially women working beneath men and the power imbalances there, and how women aren't pawns or any less able to do corporate work than men. <br /><br />So I'm conflicted. Christina Lauren definitely has written stronger books with characters I've related to much more (there is a bit of a polished gleam on all of this book's characters--probably from their origination in fanfiction--that makes them a bit untouchable), but I'm still surprised that this book was pretty enjoyable. Dare I say it, but I might just have to read its sequels, as well.</span>
  <a data-text-id="12213333276191965236" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">

<span id="freeTextContainer9336639989955457212">4.5 stars<br/><br/>I know I'm way late to this party! Like 5 years late. But as the saying goes, better late than never.<br/><br/>Looking back I have no idea why I never picked this book up. I've heard about this series for years now but somehow I never felt the urge to read it until yesterday. On top of that, I bought this book in December 2014 and it has been sitting on my kindle, waiting for me to get my act together. WORST - I didn't even know I had it until I tried to download it from the library a few days ag</span>
  <span id="freeText9336639989955457212" style="display:none">4.5 stars<br /><br />I know I'm way late to this party! Like 5 years late. But as the saying goes, better late than never.<br /><br />Looking back I have no idea why I never picked this book up. I've heard about this series for years now but somehow I never felt the urge to read it until yesterday. On top of that, I bought this book in December 2014 and it has been sitting on my kindle, waiting for me to get my act together. WORST - I didn't even know I had it until I tried to download it from the library a few days ago - true story!!!!<br /><br />So, let's get to this review.<br /><br />I love, let's change that into ADORE office romances. It is one of my most favorite trope. Add a jerk and I'm in HEAVEN!!!!! TJ cracked up when she heard that I was finally reading it. She knew that I would love it. SIGH!!!<br /><br />And yes - I LOVED IT!!!<br /><br />Beautiful Bastard had everything I enjoy in an office romance. A jerk of a boss, lot's of banter and pushing buttons on BOTH SIDES!!! It's not just him that pushed buttons, she teased him non-stop and I absolutely adored it!!<br /><br />The chemistry was through the roof. And I couldn't believe what Bennett and Chloe got up to behind closed doors. Both were strong and smart people and were matched on many levels. They actually enjoyed their little office spat - of course neither would admit to it. I have a weakness for witty and smart characters that are not afraid to take what is offered and go after what they want and Bennett and Chloe fit that bill to perfection.<br /><br />So if you love office romances, as well as sexy times on the desk, at the window, in the car and stairwell, and you love your hero to be a lovable jerk - this book is for you.<br /><br />Beautiful Bastard was sexy, steamy and utterly addicting. I'm hooked and I'm not kidding, I went straight to my library and already downloaded 4 more books in this series.<br /><br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="9336639989955457212" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('EWS9h91o5RYX3cqFIkc0fIUo82vyq5TJoHp1KD2QC2cefeXdTeZTWj9cgGJE+5VUSHGAgZRe+WKmAkEjOZH30Q==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('JnlQ0t75NEydAWpcfKFgNvA7vIvjLaJvk6udGIYYMOkpYAiITneCALWAILsaHcEePWLPYYXYz8SV06kTghnMXw==')})
  }

Thanks to paper-thin walls and the guy\'s athletic prowess, she can hear not just his bed banging against the wall but the ecstatic response of what seems (as loud night after loud night goes by) like an endless parade of women. And since Caroline is currently on a self-imposed dating hiatus, and her neighbor is clearly lethally attractive to women, she finds her fantasies keep her awake even longer than the noise. So when the wallbanging threatens to literally bounce her out of bed, Caroline, clad in sexual frustration and a pink baby-doll nightie, confronts Simon Parker, her heard-but-never-seen neighbor. The tension between them is as thick as the walls are thin, and the results just as mixed. Suddenly, Caroline is finding she may have discovered a whole new definition of neighborly...\n\nIn a delicious mix of silly and steamy, Alice Clayton dishes out a hot and hilarious tale of
